drop database if exists DBMS_PROJECT_2;
create database DBMS_PROJECT_2;
use DBMS_PROJECT_2;


create table HANGAR(
	hangar_num int primary key auto_increment,
    capacity SMALLINT,
    location varchar(4)
);

create table AIRPLANE(
	reg_num varchar(30) primary key,
    of_type varchar(20),
    hangar_num int,
    foreign key(hangar_num) references HANGAR(hangar_num)
);

create table PLANE_TYPE(
	model_number varchar(20) primary key,
    capacity MEDIUMINT,
    weight double
);

create table _OWNER(
	owner_id int primary key auto_increment
);

create table PERSON(/*Sub type of owner*/
	person_num int primary key,
    fname varchar(20),
    lname varchar(30),
    /*(000)-000-0000*/
    owner_phone varchar(15), /*0-000-000-0000*/
    ssn varchar(10),
    foreign key(person_num) references _OWNER(owner_id)
);

create table OWNS(
 p_airplane varchar(30),
 p_date date,
 o_id int,
 
 primary key(p_airplane, p_date),
 foreign key(p_airplane) references AIRPLANE(reg_num),
 foreign key(o_id) references _OWNER(owner_id)
);

create table EMPLOYEE(/*subtype of person*/
	employee_num int primary key,
	salary DECIMAL(13, 4),
	foreign key(employee_num) references PERSON(person_num)
);

create table CORPORATION(/*subtype of owner*/
	corporation_num int primary key,
    name varchar(40),
    /*(000)-000-0000*/
    owner_phone varchar(15), /*0-000-000-0000*/
    foreign key(corporation_num) references _OWNER(owner_id)
);

create table PILOT(/*sub type of person*/
	pilot_num int primary key,
    lic_num  varchar(20),
    salary DECIMAL(13, 4)
);
create table RESTRICTION(/*Describes types of resctrictions*/
	r_code varchar(6) primary key,
    descript TEXT
);
create table PILOT_RESTRICTIONS( /*Lists restrictions a pilot has*/
	pilot_num int,
    r_code varchar(6),
    primary key(pilot_num, r_code),
    foreign key(pilot_num) references PILOT(pilot_num),
    foreign key(r_code) references RESTRICTION(r_code)
);

create table WORK_CODE( /*Describes some job preformed on a plane for service*/
	work_code varchar(6) primary key,
    descript text
);

create table SERVICE( /*Says **what** work was done on a plane*/
    service_id int primary key auto_increment,
	work_code varchar(6),
    reg_num varchar(30),
    foreign key(reg_num) references AIRPLANE(reg_num)
);


create table MAINTAIN( /*Says **who** did work on a plane **when** */
	employee_num int,
    service_id int,
    shift_in datetime,
    shift_out datetime,
    
    primary key(employee_num, service_id),
    foreign key(employee_num) references EMPLOYEE(employee_num),
    foreign key(service_id) references SERVICE(service_id)
);

create table FLIES( /*What pilots can fly what types of planes, ex: Pilots trained for small air craft should not fly the 720*/
	pilot_num int,
    plane_type varchar(20),
    
    primary key(pilot_num, plane_type),
    foreign key(pilot_num) references PILOT(pilot_num),
    foreign key(plane_type) references PLANE_TYPE(model_number)
);

create table WORKS_ON( /*What employees are allowed to work on what types of planes*/
	employee_num int,
    plane_type varchar(20),
    primary key( employee_num, plane_type ),
    foreign key(employee_num) references EMPLOYEE(employee_num),
    foreign key(plane_type) references PLANE_TYPE(model_number)
);
